#1

11.02.2019, 22:24
Hello, I made this map for a old Roleplay server. But now, I have decided to release in the community for devs has interest on it. So, thanks for the view and enjoy this map.

PS: The .rar attach files contain the code and the .db file if you are interested in changing textures or mapping in texture-studio.

• This is a clean map with only SA-MP/GTA SA objects;
• The draw distance is default 300.0, but its is possible change, and I recommend it for more RP experience;
• You have 2 options of choise, the Cluck Bell Version and Teen Green Bottle Bar, I like more the Cluckin' Bell for RP experience (Idk if in California you can drink alcohol in exterior).














More Pictures: https://imgur.com/a/G4Og5ms

Idlewood Donuts


More Pictures:
https://i.postimg.cc/vB4K5Qpk/sa-mp-281.png
https://i.postimg.cc/QM4PBBnc/sa-mp-282.png
